Foreword to Il, Bande. The pressure of the II. volume of my directory is still 2u
Begun at the end of 1905. Since then, of course, there has been one
quite significant number of works appeared in which both
new species of Homoptera have been described, as well as new data on the
geographic distribution of already known forms. In addition, I lived in Tashkent until the end of May 1906, where some
Papers, from various scientific journals
were inaccessible. For these reasons it turned out in my
work a series of omissions and lilies that I particularly
their sitting and corrections at the end of the present one
Bandes (pp. 382-456) considered necessary. are arranged
them according to the following plan: According to the number which the side of the ver-
sign means, the number is in brackets, followed by the
Name of the species to which the adjuncts belong and, finally, the
the latter, preceded by the letter S (i.e. systematics,
synonymy) if new citations or synonymy are involved
delt, and the letter V (i.e. distribution) if they contain data about
contain the geographical distribution of the species. in front of the forms
which have not been mentioned before, or before those in which
the earlier given text has been replaced by a completely different one
is, the number is not in parentheses. All work in
»List of literature used* (Vol. I, pp. X — LXXIV)
which have not been mentioned are in a special supplement list
compiled, which can be found behind this foreword. The number of all Paliactic, as well as especially the Russian
hen Homopteran genera and species in the present volume

V. Belgica. P. 377, (1601). Tr. acutipennis Zerr. V. Belgica. P, 379, (1612). Tr. viridula Zerr. V.Hungaria. Alphabetical register

ll. Band. The names adopted in the register are in ordinary script, the
Synonyms printed in italics. After each species or variety name follows in brackets-
mers the designation of the genus to which they are born and then the number
under which they are in the directory. If the same shape also in the
sitting is mentioned, then after the digit that designates the serial number,
the reference to the side of the seats, with the side designation starting with the
letter p (pagina) is marked. If a species does not appear in the text,
but is only mentioned in the additions, the index contains the page number first
and then the consecutive number. For generic and other names
higher systematic groups and their synonyms is only referred to the page
grasslands. To save space, each type is only used once in the register
mentioned, albeit at different times in different genera
